app1.add_handler(CommandHandler(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"start"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span></span><span> u, c: u.message.reply_text(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Bot 1 ishda"</span></span><span>)))

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># 2-bot</span></span><span>
app2 = Application.builder().token(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"TOKEN_2"</span></span><span>).build()
app2.add_handler(CommandHandler(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"start"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span></span><span> u, c: u.message.reply_text(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Bot 2 ishda"</span></span><span>)))

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># 3-bot</span></span><span>
app3 = Application.builder().token(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"TOKEN_3"</span></span><span>).build()
app3.add_handler(CommandHandler(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"start"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span></span><span> u, c: u.message.reply_text(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Bot 3 ishda"</span></span><span>)))

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># 4-bot</span></span><span>
app4 = Application.builder().token(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"TOKEN_4"</span></span><span>).build()
app4.add_handler(CommandHandler(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"start"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span></span><span> u, c: u.message.reply_text(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Bot 4 ishda"</span></span><span>)))

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Barchasini birgalikda ishga tushurish</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> asyncio

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">async</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">run_all</span></span><span>():
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span></span><span> asyncio.gather(
        app1.run_polling(),
        app2.run_polling(),
        app3.run_polling(),
        app4.run_polling()
    )

asyncio.run(run_all())
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
